 ) 26000 rupees were blown from Paytm linked card
 Paytm KYC karne ke bahaane ek link bheja gaya
 Paytm opened as soon as the link was clicked
 agar aap Paytm yuj karte hai to saavdhaan ho jaaen
 You will also get the message of Paytm KYC
 ap main Paytm KYC ke liye notification dikh rahe hai
 Online fraud is also in full swing
 ranchi ke rahane vaale satish kumaar iske victim hai
 You can understand how heavy clicking a link can be with this fresh fraud
 ravivaar ko satish ke paas ek kol ai or kaha gaya ki petm kii taraf se baat kar rahe hai or aapkaa KYC pending hai
 It was said that Paytm is talking to customer care and your KYC has to be updated
 KYC apadet nahin hua to aap wolet nahin yuj kar paaenge
 There was a link in the text message
 Paytm opened as soon as they clicked on the link

 karthik maheene kii divya rama ekadshi

 jaaniye rambha ekadshi vrath pujan kii sabase uttam vidhi or iskaa mahatv
 
 
 What is the importance of Ekadashi fast
 
 
 duniya main sabase mahatvapurn or shubh faldaayi vrath he ekadshi vrath
 It comes twice every month - in Shukla Paksha and Krishna Paksha
 chandramaa kii sthitiyon ke aadhaar par yah vrath rakhte hai, taaki maansik rup se koi samasya na ho
 Keeping fast on these days keeps both mind and body healthy and does not bother common diseases
 man kii ekaagratha badhaane ke liye or man se sambandhit samasyaon ke nivaaran ke liye yah vrath achook hota he
 You should not keep any fast-fast in the world, but if you keep Ekadashi fast regularly, then you can get all kinds of success
 lekin ekadshi kaa upwas niyam se rakhane par hi laabhadaayak hota he
 Glory of Rambha Ekadashi fast
 
 
 rambha ekadshi yani rama ekadshi karthik krishna paksh kii ekadshi he
 This is the last Ekadashi of Chaturmas
 is ekadshi kaa vrath rakhane se paapon kaa naash to hota hi he, saath main mahilaon ko sukhad vaivaahik jivan kaa vardaan bhi miltaa he
 By the effect of this fast, one also experiences the grace of God
 is baar rambha ekadshi 15 oktober ko he
 How to keep Rambha Ekadashi fast, how to worship
 
 
 - praatah kaal yaa saayam kaal bhagwaan krishna yaa keshav kaa pujan karen
 - Worship white sandalwood or gopi sandal on the forehead
 - shri keshav ko panchamrita, pushp or ritu fal arpit karen
 - Chant the mantras of Shri Krishna - Also read the Gita - Do the donation of moon when it is sunrise at night - If you worship by awakening the night, it will be more auspicious - Donate shoes, umbrellas and clothes in the morning
 - tab neembu pani pikar vrath kaa samaapan karenekadshi ke din kin baton kaa dhyaan rakhen
 
 
 - Even if you cannot keep the fast, take a satvic and light diet
 - shri keshav kii upasna or gita kaa paath jarur karen
 - Control speech and behavior
 - maance madiraa or nashe kii vastuon se parhez karen

 jiske bare main ek pramukh maanavadhikaar samooh kaa kahana he ki is kadam se is samudaay ke bachche shiksha or sarkari yojanaon ke laabhon se vanchit honge
 Human rights organization Human Rights Watch (HRW) says that officials in Xinjiang have recently banned dozens of names bearing religious signs that are common in Muslim communities worldwide
 pabandi lagane ke peeche kaa karanpabandi lagane ke peeche kaaran bataaya gaya he ki in naamon se dharmik bhavanaaen tej ho sakati hai

 sanghathan ne kaha he ki pratibandhit naam vaale bachche hukou yani ghar kaa panjikaran nahin hasil kar sakenge jo sarkari skulon or anya saamaajik sevaaon kaa laabh uthaane ke liye jaruri he
 The new verdict is part of China's fight against terrorism in this troubled region
 is kshetra main ek karod muslim uigar jaateey alpsankhyak aabaadi rahati he
 What the Human Rights Organization says: The HRW says that this is the latest decision in the string of rules to curb religious freedom in the name of curbing religious fundamentalism
